    When we stood against you Wyrmcomers, we fell. When you stood in our homes against the wicked spirits that you'd brought with you, you fell. Now we stand together, and if our totems are willing, we will not fall. Our cunning and your savagery, our wisdom+ and your speed— it. makes my heart burn to say that we need one another, but there is no other option. Come. Let us shed blood together. — Weeping Stone, Uktena Philodox
